name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Panoramic Suite A (With balcony)
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Business travelers
info:9 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted March 22, 2024
msg:The Linghai Villa Hotel has a long history. I heard from the staff that it was built in 1919 and was the private villa of Guo Chunyang, one of the four sugar kings in Southeast Asia at that time.
The villa is a three-story building, and the linked arched porches freeze the century-old Xiamen Bay seascape one by one. On the first floor, you can enjoy the courtyard, and the layers of courtyards are like a small maze. On the second floor, you can enjoy the light, lean on the railing and gather, as high as the trees, and the sea in the distance is looming. On the third floor, you can enjoy the sea from sunrise to sunset, and never miss it.
The staff is warm and thoughtful, and the breakfast is exquisite, nutritious and delicious! They also considerately upgraded me to a sea view room, haha!

posted:Posted February 15, 2024
msg:Linghai Hotel is a chain hotel in Gulangyu Island. The hotel we stayed in is located near Sunlight Rock and Shuzhuang Garden. It is a single-family villa and is very quiet. I booked a sea view room, which can directly face the sea and enjoy the blooming flowers in spring. The room is clean and tidy, and the bathroom and balcony are spacious. It is very pleasant to listen to the sound of the waves and taste the aroma of black tea on the balcony.
The hotel also has many hidden benefits, such as you can borrow sand digging tools for free, and the beach is a 5-minute walk away. Children can just spend the whole afternoon digging. Afternoon tea is provided every day, including 2 small cakes and a pot of tea. There is also free laundry service, both dry cleaning and drying, which is very convenient.
On the day you first arrive at the hotel, the hotel provides free luggage transportation to the hotel. However, you will have to pay extra to transport your luggage on the return trip.

There are ice-cold drinks at the front desk to quench your thirst. It is very comfortable to have a drink at the hotel. The waiter will help carry the luggage to the room.

Facilities: The hotel was renovated from an old building, and the overall style of the ancient building is retained. The facilities in the hotel rooms are relatively new, because it is on an island, and the water pipes are laid. If there are many people using hot water, you may have to wait. meeting.


Hygiene: Hygiene is very good, but because of the lush vegetation nearby, there are many mosquitoes. The hotel provides mosquito repellent water, so remember to spray it.


Environment: The hotel itself has a very good environment. It is very close to Sunlight Rock, Zheng Chenggong Memorial Hall, Shuzhuang Garden, International Lettering Art Museum (the address on the hand-drawn map is wrong), Aberdeen Back Beach, and Longtou Road Snack Street.

Transportation: It is strongly recommended to steal from Sanqiutian Pier. The road over to Neicuoao Pier is too difficult.


Breakfast: Breakfast is in the form of a set meal. There are not too many types. It is quite exquisite and tastes okay. There is also milk, soy milk, coffee, fruit and bread.

Afternoon tea: Before 16 o'clock, the taste is quite good, and the photos are not bad. You can still try it if it comes with a set meal, but I don't recommend buying it yourself.

Taking photos: If you are given photos, I think 5 photos are enough. If you have the skills, you can actually take photos yourself.

To sum up, the hotel is very good overall and I recommend everyone to give it a try.
